Contributors

These are all the Milky Way Project volunteers who contributed to our first data release (DR1). Visit our data and explore pages for more information. We also have a page explaining the people that make up our science team.

The images on this page are the 100 most favourited Milky Way Project images from DR1. Click on any of them to learn more.
